<h1 class="header"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Jurassic World</span>
<span class="nobr">(<a href="/year/2015/?ref_=tt_ov_inf">2015</a>)</span>
</h1>
<div class="infobar">
<a href="/genre/Action?ref_=tt_ov_inf"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Action</span></a>
<span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="/genre/Adventure?ref_=tt_ov_inf"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Adventure</span></a>
<span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="/genre/Sci-Fi?ref_=tt_ov_inf"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Sci-Fi</span></a>
                -
            <span class="nobr">
<a href="/title/tt0369610/releaseinfo?ref_=tt_ov_inf+" title="See all release dates"> 11 June 2015<meta content="2015-06-11" itemprop="datePublished"/>
(Germany)
</a> </span>
</div>
<div class="star-box giga-star">
<div class="star-box-rating-widget">
<div class="rating rating-list">
<div class="rating-ineligible">
<a href="/help/show_leaf?votestopfaq&amp;ref_=tt_ov_rt">Not yet released</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="star-box-details" itemprop="aggregateRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/AggregateRating">
            (voting begins after release)
 
    </div>
<div class="clear"></div>
</div>
<p></p>
<p itemprop="description">
Twenty-two years after the events of <a href="/title/tt0107290">Jurassic Park</a> (1993), Isla Nublar now features a fully functioning dinosaur theme park, Jurassic World, as originally envisioned by John Hammond. After 10 years of operation and visitor rates declining, in order to fulfill a corporate mandate, a new attraction is created to re-spark visitor's interest, which backfires horribly.</p>
<p></p>
<div class="txt-block" itemprop="director" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
<h4 class="inline">Director:</h4>
<a href="/name/nm1119880/?ref_=tt_ov_dr" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Colin Trevorrow</span></a>
</div>
<div class="txt-block" itemprop="creator" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
<h4 class="inline">Writers:</h4>
<a href="/name/nm2081046/?ref_=tt_ov_wr" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Derek Connolly</span></a>               (screenplay), 
<a href="/name/nm1119880/?ref_=tt_ov_wr" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Colin Trevorrow</span></a>               (screenplay), <a href="fullcredits?ref_=tt_ov_wr#writers">1 more credit</a>
    </div>
<div class="txt-block" itemprop="actors" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
<h4 class="inline">Stars:</h4>
<a href="/name/nm0695435/?ref_=tt_ov_st" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Chris Pratt</span></a>, 
<a href="/name/nm0339460/?ref_=tt_ov_st" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Judy Greer</span></a>, 
<a href="/name/nm1339223/?ref_=tt_ov_st" itemprop="url"><span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Ty Simpkins</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>
<span class="see-more inline nobr">
<a href="fullcredits?ref_=tt_ov_st_sm" itemprop="url"> See full cast and crew</a>

</div>

<div class="article" id="titleStoryLine">
<span class="rightcornerlink">
<a href="/register/login?why=edit&amp;ref_=tt_stry" rel="login">Edit</a>

<h2>Storyline</h2>
<div class="inline canwrap" itemprop="description">
<p>
Twenty-two years after the events of <a href="/title/tt0107290?ref_=tt_stry_pl">Jurassic Park</a> (1993), Isla Nublar now features a fully functioning dinosaur theme park, Jurassic World, as originally envisioned by John Hammond. After 10 years of operation and visitor rates declining, in order to fulfill a corporate mandate, a new attraction is created to re-spark visitor's interest, which backfires horribly.            </p>
</div>
<span class="see-more inline">
<a href="/title/tt0369610/plotsummary?ref_=tt_stry_pl">Plot Summary</a>
<span>|</span>
<a href="/title/tt0369610/synopsis?ref_=tt_stry_pl">Add Synopsis</a>
</span>
<hr/>

<div class="article" id="titleDidYouKnow">

</span>
<h2>Did You Know?</h2>
<div class="txt-block" id="trivia">
<h4>Trivia</h4>


The first Jurassic Park film to not have animatronic dinosaurs created by <a href="/name/nm0935644?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Stan Winston</a>, as he passed away in 2008. Instead the animatronics were created by effects studio Legacy Effects, a company formed from Winston's former workshop staff.        <a class="nobr" href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv">See more</a>  
    </div>
<hr/>
